Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

| SessionLogHandler::HandleSaveSessionLogRequest | [1] is a WebUI message callback, it will show a file dialog. After select file, | SessionLogHandler::FileSelected | will be called, it will post a task with | this | raw pointer in [2]. If attack close the chrome://diagnostics before the posted task executed, |SessionLogHandler| (i.e., |this| pointer) will be freed, causing UAF when the posted task executed in | SessionLogHandler::CreateSessionLog |.



<span class="line"><!---->| SessionLogHandler::HandleSaveSessionLogRequest | [1] is a WebUI message callback, it will show a file dialog. After select file, | SessionLogHandler::FileSelected | will be called, it will post a task with | this | raw pointer in [2]. If attack close the chrome://diagnostics before the posted task executed, |SessionLogHandler| (i.e., |this| pointer) will be freed, causing UAF when the posted task executed in | SessionLogHandler::CreateSessionLog |.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1]



<span class="line"><!---->[1]<!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/diagnostics_ui/backend/session_log_handler.cc;drc=53ca2582059ccb3d3005a8b8e56e595b6b1f47e5;l=198



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/diagnostics_ui/backend/session_log_handler.cc;drc=53ca2582059ccb3d3005a8b8e56e595b6b1f47e5;l=198"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/diagnostics_ui/backend/session_log_handler.cc;drc=53ca2582059ccb3d3005a8b8e56e595b6b1f47e5;l=198<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





[2]



<span class="line"><!---->[2]<!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/diagnostics_ui/backend/session_log_handler.cc;l=106-111;drc=53ca2582059ccb3d3005a8b8e56e595b6b1f47e5



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/diagnostics_ui/backend/session_log_handler.cc;l=106-111;drc=53ca2582059ccb3d3005a8b8e56e595b6b1f47e5"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/diagnostics_ui/backend/session_log_handler.cc;l=106-111;drc=53ca2582059ccb3d3005a8b8e56e595b6b1f47e5<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





    task_runner_->PostTaskAndReplyWithResult(



<span class="line"><!---->    task_runner_-&gt;PostTaskAndReplyWithResult(<!----></span>



<br>





        FROM_HERE,



<span class="line"><!---->        FROM_HERE,<!----></span>



<br>





        base::BindOnce(&SessionLogHandler::CreateSessionLog,



<span class="line"><!---->        base::BindOnce(&amp;SessionLogHandler::CreateSessionLog,<!----></span>



<br>





                       base::Unretained(this), path), // [2]



<span class="line"><!---->                       base::Unretained(this), path), // [2]<!----></span>



<br>





        base::BindOnce(&SessionLogHandler::OnSessionLogCreated, weak_ptr_,



<span class="line"><!---->        base::BindOnce(&amp;SessionLogHandler::OnSessionLogCreated, weak_ptr_,<!----></span>



<br>





                       path));



<span class="line"><!---->                       path));<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





Hence attacker could exploit it by the following chain:



<span class="line"><!---->Hence attacker could exploit it by the following chain:<!----></span>



<br>





1. execute JS script `chrome.send("saveSessionLog", [""]);`  in chrome://diagnostics ( this could achieve by combining with a UXSS),  or user click saveSessionLog button



<span class="line"><!---->1. execute JS script `chrome.send("saveSessionLog", [""]);`  in chrome://diagnostics ( this could achieve by combining with a UXSS),  or user click saveSessionLog button<!----></span>



<br>





2. closing the chrome://diagnostics page by `window.close()` (in order to free SessionLogHandler), after user select a file. (this may need a race, to stable trigger it, attacker could post a lot of tasks to delay the execution of CreateSessionLog)



<span class="line"><!---->2. closing the chrome://diagnostics page by `window.close()` (in order to free SessionLogHandler), after user select a file. (this may need a race, to stable trigger it, attacker could post a lot of tasks to delay the execution of CreateSessionLog)<!----></span>



<br>





3. UAF occurs in SessionLogHandler::CreateSessionLog when it was posted  (SessionLogHandler is freed now, |this| is an invalid pointer)



<span class="line"><!---->3. UAF occurs in SessionLogHandler::CreateSessionLog when it was posted  (SessionLogHandler is freed now, |this| is an invalid pointer)<!----></span>

Due to an issue with the monorail wizard workflow, this issue was not originally labeled as a security bug and, therefore, this issue did not make it to the security team bug queue for triage. This wizard workflow issue was just discovered today, updating accordingly now. 



<span class="line"><!---->Due to an issue with the monorail wizard workflow, this issue was not originally labeled as a security bug and, therefore, this issue did not make it to the security team bug queue for triage. <br>





Since this is reporting a potential UAF, updating as security bug. OS already set to OS=Chrome so this should now make it into the Chrome OS security triage queue for Chrome OS triage.

It looks like for the UaF to occur the DiagnosticsApp has to be closed while the CreateSessionLog function is running.  I was only able to get the failure to trigger by adding a busy loop in the CreateSessionLog function to give time for the task to start before attempting to close the window.  The scenario described in #2 to build up a task queue does sound plausible I'm not sure how it would be triggered given that SessionLogHandler has its own task runner. I have not been able to get either scenario to trigger in a test.



<span class="line"><!---->It looks like for the UaF to occur the DiagnosticsApp has to be closed while the CreateSessionLog function is running.  I was only able to get the failure to trigger by adding a busy loop in the CreateSessionLog function to give time for the task to start before attempting to close the window.  The scenario described in #2 to build up a task queue does sound plausible I'm not sure how it would be triggered given that SessionLogHandler has its own task runner. I have not been able to get either scenario to trigger in a test.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





IIUC, `base::Unretained(this)` is used instead of a WeakPtr becase WeakPtr can only be used with void functions. From manual testing, if the destruction of SessionLogHandler occurred before the task started then using a WeakPtr and changing CreateSessiongLog to be a void function will keep the task from starting. Once the task is running it's too late and you can still get the UaF.



<span class="line"><!---->IIUC, `base::Unretained(this)` is used instead of a WeakPtr becase WeakPtr can only be used with void functions. From manual testing, if the destruction of SessionLogHandler occurred before the task started then using a WeakPtr and changing CreateSessiongLog to be a void function will keep the task from starting. Once the task is running it's too late and you can still get the UaF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What might work here is handling the content gathering prior to launching the task so that CreateSessionLog takes the `std::vector<std::string> pieces` as a param to make the task "self-contained".  I'm not sure if there is another way of ensuring all tasks complete or are canceled before destroying SessionLogHandler.



<span class="line"><!---->What might work here is handling the content gathering prior to launching the task so that CreateSessionLog takes the `std::vector&lt;std::string&gt; pieces` as a param to make the task "self-contained".  I'm not sure if there is another way of ensuring all tasks complete or are canceled before destroying SessionLogHandler.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The current implementation (starting M104 with flag enabled), DiagnosticsLogController's lifetime is aligned with the ash::Shell so the UaF should not happen.



<span class="line"><!---->The current implementation (starting M104 with flag enabled), DiagnosticsLogController's lifetime is aligned with the ash::Shell so the UaF should not happen.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>
